The function `check_fit_check_is_fitted` in `sklearn/utils/estimator_checks.py` validates this behavior for all estimators. It is used in: `sklearn/base.py`, `sklearn/dummy.py`, `sklearn/pipeline.py`, `sklearn/isotonic.py`, `sklearn/multiclass.py`, `sklearn/svm/_base.py`, `sklearn/mixture/_base.py`, `sklearn/model_selection/_classification_threshold.py`, and many more.\\n\\n**3.
